 safer C code [ 40 ]

   — — — — — — — — — — — — — — — — — — - 
   1       Follow the rules you ’ve read a hundred times 
   2       Use enumerations as error types 
   3       Expect to fail 
   4       Check input values : never trust a stranger 
   5       Write once , read many times 
   6       When in doubt , leave it out 
   7       Use the right tools
